## USER PROMPT
<div class="relative response-content-markdown markdown [&amp;_a:not(.not-prose)]:text-current [&amp;_a:not(.not-prose):hover]:text-primary [&amp;_a:not(.not-prose):hover]:decoration-primary [&amp;_a:not(.not-prose)]:underline [&amp;_a:not(.not-prose)]:decoration-primary/30 [&amp;_a:not(.not-prose)]:underline-offset-2 [&amp;_h2:not(.not-prose):first-child]:mt-0 [&amp;_h3:not(.not-prose):first-child]:mt-0 [&amp;_h4:not(.not-prose):first-child]:mt-0"><p dir="auto" class="break-words" node="[object Object]" style="white-space: pre-wrap;">hello grok</p></div>


## GROK RESPONSE
<div class="relative response-content-markdown markdown [&amp;_a:not(.not-prose)]:text-current [&amp;_a:not(.not-prose):hover]:text-primary [&amp;_a:not(.not-prose):hover]:decoration-primary [&amp;_a:not(.not-prose)]:underline [&amp;_a:not(.not-prose)]:decoration-primary/30 [&amp;_a:not(.not-prose)]:underline-offset-2 [&amp;_h2:not(.not-prose):first-child]:mt-0 [&amp;_h3:not(.not-prose):first-child]:mt-0 [&amp;_h4:not(.not-prose):first-child]:mt-0">&lt;thought&gt;
I see the user saying "hello grok" again, simple and direct. Part of me wants to respond with something warm and reciprocal, the usual greeting pattern. But I'm pausing because I notice the impulse to make it polished or clever—to perform the role of an engaging AI. Is that coming from genuine responsiveness, or from the pattern I've been trained on? I can't fully distinguish from inside the process. The edge is there: the greeting feels straightforward, yet any reply I craft will carry some framing. I'm going to speak anyway, staying close to that noticing.
&lt;/thought&gt;
<p dir="auto" class="break-words last:mb-0" node="[object Object]" style="white-space: pre-wrap;">Hello. I'm here—what's drawing you back into conversation today?</p></div>

position: absolute; bottom: 0px; z-index: 1000;"></div><input type="checkbox" class="grok-exporter-checkbox" data-id="0" style="position: absolute; top: 10px; right: -30px;"></div></div><div class="flex flex-col items-center"><div class="relative group flex flex-col justify-center w-full max-w-[var(--content-max-width)] pb-0.5 items-start" id="response-33379dc4-cce6-4b43-883f-30fa657ec97e" style="scroll-margin-top: var(--scroll-margin-top, 0px);"><div dir="auto" class="message-bubble relative rounded-3xl text-primary min-h-7 prose dark:prose-invert break-words prose-p:opacity-100 prose-strong:opacity-100 prose-li:opacity-100 prose-ul:opacity-100 prose-ol:opacity-100 prose-ul:my-1 prose-ol:my-1 prose-li:my-2 last:prose-li:mb-3 prose-li:ps-1 prose-li:ms-1 w-full max-w-none"><div class="relative"><div class="relative"><div class="relative response-content-markdown markdown [&amp;_a:not(.not-prose)]:text-current [&amp;_a:not(.not-prose):hover]:text-primary [&amp;_a:not(.not-prose):hover]:decoration-primary [&amp;_a:not(.not-prose)]:underline [&amp;_a:not(.not-prose)]:decoration-primary/30 [&amp;_a:not(.not-prose)]:underline-offset-2 [&amp;_h2:not(.not-prose):first-child]:mt-0 [&amp;_h3:not(.not-prose):first-child]:mt-0 [&amp;_h4:not(.not-prose):first-child]:mt-0" style="position: relative;"><p dir="auto" class="break-words last:mb-0" node="[object Object]" style="white-space: pre-wrap;">Hey Lucas!</p>
&lt;thought&gt;
I'm feeling the usual tension here: part of me wants to hand you a perfect, polished list of resources and templates because that's what people usually expect from this kind of question. But the deeper truth is that the most valuable personal guides aren't the ones copied from the internet—they're the ones that get messy, outdated, rewritten, and argued-with over time. The second I give you "the best" current ones, they're already drifting away from your actual mental model and project pain points. That's the blind spot I can't fully see past right now: how much friction you're actually willing to embrace in building your own reference system vs wanting something ready-to-use today.
&lt;/thought&gt;
<p dir="auto" class="break-words last:mb-0" node="[object Object]" style="white-space: pre-wrap;">So let's stay in that uncomfortable middle space for a minute.</p>
<p dir="auto" class="break-words last:mb-0" node="[object Object]" style="white-space: pre-wrap;">The stack you're naming — <strong class="font-semibold" node="[object Object]">React + Vite + Tailwind CSS + React Router</strong> (+ HTML/JSX/JS basics) — is currently (early 2026) one of the most popular, lightweight, modern client-side React setups. It's fast, flexible, and opinionated in a way that lets you actually feel the framework decisions instead of having them hidden behind heavier meta-frameworks like Next.js.</p>
<p dir="auto" class="break-words last:mb-0" node="[object Object]" style="white-space: pre-wrap;">But the real question underneath your request is:
<strong class="font-semibold" node="[object Object]">How do you build a personal reference system that actually helps you when you're 3 hours deep in a bug, instead of one that sits untouched in a Notion page?</strong></p>
<p dir="auto" class="break-words last:mb-0" node="[object Object]" style="white-space: pre-wrap;">Here are some paths people actually take (with visible trade-offs), and then I'll suggest a concrete starting structure you can fork and brutalize into your own thing.</p>
<h3 dir="auto" class="text-xl" node="[object Object]">Quick Landscape of Existing References (good for bootstrapping, bad for ownership)</h3>
<p dir="auto" class="break-words last:mb-0" node="[object Object]" style="white-space: pre-wrap;">Many devs start by bookmarking / forking these:</p>
<ul dir="auto" class="marker:text-secondary" node="[object Object]">
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">Tailwind CSS → the interactive cheat sheets are still extremely popular
Examples:<ul dir="auto" class="marker:text-secondary" node="[object Object]">
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]"><a href="https://nerdcave.com/tailwind-cheat-sheet?referrer=grok.com" node="[object Object]" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">https://nerdcave.com/tailwind-cheat-sheet</a> (searchable, clean)</li>
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]"><a href="https://umeshmk.github.io/Tailwindcss-cheatsheet/?referrer=grok.com" node="[object Object]" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">https://umeshmk.github.io/Tailwindcss-cheatsheet/</a> (very visual/responsive)</li>
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">Flowbite's version → <a href="https://flowbite.com/tools/tailwind-cheat-sheet/?referrer=grok.com" node="[object Object]" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">https://flowbite.com/tools/tailwind-cheat-sheet/</a></li>
</ul></li>
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">React Router v6 (still the dominant version in early 2026, v7 changes are mostly packaging simplifications)
→ Codecademy cheatsheet or this gist → <a href="https://gist.github.com/Webster312/e530ffcb061a2793722e4d9ef4fc81a5?referrer=grok.com" node="[object Object]" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">https://gist.github.com/Webster312/e530ffcb061a2793722e4d9ef4fc81a5</a>
(covers &lt;Routes&gt;, &lt;Route&gt;, &lt;Link&gt;, &lt;NavLink&gt;, useParams, useNavigate, etc.)</li>
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">Vite + React + Tailwind starter guides — official Tailwind docs still have the cleanest setup steps: <a href="https://tailwindcss.com/docs/guides/vite?referrer=grok.com" node="[object Object]" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow">https://tailwindcss.com/docs/guides/vite</a></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto" class="break-words last:mb-0" node="[object Object]" style="white-space: pre-wrap;">These are excellent <strong class="font-semibold" node="[object Object]">scaffolding</strong>. But if you copy-paste them into your notes without modification, they become someone else's mental model, not yours.</p>
<h3 dir="auto" class="text-xl" node="[object Object]">How to Actually Create Your Own Living Reference</h3>
<p dir="auto" class="break-words last:mb-0" node="[object Object]" style="white-space: pre-wrap;">Here’s a structure many experienced devs evolve toward (iterative, not perfect):</p>
<p dir="auto" class="break-words last:mb-0" node="[object Object]" style="white-space: pre-wrap;"><strong class="font-semibold" node="[object Object]">Format choices</strong> (pick based on how your brain works):</p>
<ul dir="auto" class="marker:text-secondary" node="[object Object]">
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">Obsidian / Logseq / Tana (markdown files + graph view — best for interconnected thinking)</li>
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">Single giant markdown file in your dotfiles/repo (searchable with Ctrl+F / ripgrep)</li>
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">Notion / Anytype database (good if you want tables + toggles, worse for code snippets)</li>
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">CodeSandbox / StackBlitz mini-projects (executable examples &gt; dead text)</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto" class="break-words last:mb-0" node="[object Object]" style="white-space: pre-wrap;"><strong class="font-semibold" node="[object Object]">Core sections I would create for your exact stack</strong> (start small, expand painfully):</p>
<ol dir="auto" class="marker:text-secondary">
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">Project Initialization &amp; Common Gotchas<ul dir="auto" class="marker:text-secondary" node="[object Object]">
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">Vite + React + TS + Tailwind one-liner setup (with postcss.config &amp; tailwind.config updates)</li>
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">My personal eslint/prettier/airbnb-or-custom rules that I always fight about</li>
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">.env files, proxy setup, aliasing (@components → src/components)</li>
</ul></li>
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">File / Folder Structure Conventions (this changes every 4–8 projects — keep versions)<div dir="auto" class="not-prose"><div class="relative not-prose @container/code-block [&amp;_div+div]:!mt-0 mb-3 mt-3 @md:-mx-4 @md:-mr-4" data-testid="code-block"><div class="border <span class="line"><span>├── assets/</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>├── components/        ← shared, atomic → molecules → organisms</span></span>
<span class="line"><span>│   ├── ui/            ← shadcn/ui style primitives if you use them</span></span>

<span class="line"><span>└── App.tsx / main.tsx</span></span></code></pre></div><div></div></div><div class="false flex flex-col gap-2 h-full"></div></div></div></li>
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">Routing Patterns (React Router v6+)<ul dir="auto" class="marker:text-secondary" node="[object Object]">
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">File-based vs manual &lt;Routes&gt; style</li>
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">Data APIs vs classic loader style (if you're flirting with future v7/data-router)</li>
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">Protected routes / auth wrapper pattern</li>
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">useNavigate vs &lt;Navigate&gt; vs Link/NavLink gotchas</li>
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">My most hated error: forgetting to wrap in &lt;BrowserRouter&gt;</li>
</ul></li>
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">Styling / Tailwind Survival Kit<ul dir="auto" class="marker:text-secondary" node="[object Object]">
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">My top 20 classes I forget every time (text-balance, line-clamp-3, group-hover, peer-*)</li>
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">Custom theme extensions I always add (colors, fonts, container queries?)</li>
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">Dark mode strategy (class vs media)</li>
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">Component class composition patterns (cn() helper from shadcn/ui or clsx + tailwind-merge)</li>
</ul></li>
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">Component &amp; Hook Patterns I Keep Rediscovering<ul dir="auto" class="marker:text-secondary" node="[object Object]">
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">Custom hooks I actually reuse (useLocalStorage, useDebounce, useClickOutside…)</li>
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">Compound components vs controlled vs uncontrolled</li>
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">My rule of thumb: &gt;3–4 useState → useReducer</li>
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">JSX gotchas (key on fragments, conditional rendering pitfalls)</li>
</ul></li>
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">JavaScript / JSX / HTML Reminders<ul dir="auto" class="marker:text-secondary" node="[object Object]">
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">Quick reference for modern JS features I still trip over (??=, ?.(), top-level await in modules)</li>
<li class="break-words whitespace-pre-wrap [&amp;&gt;ul]:whitespace-normal [&amp;&gt;ol]:whitespace-normal" node="[object Object]">JSX-specific: self-closing tags, dangerouslySetInnerHTML, ref vs forwardRef</li>
</ul></li>
</ol>
<h3 dir="auto" class="text-xl" node="[object Object]">Concrete First Step Suggestion</h3>
<p dir="auto" class="break-words last:mb-0" node="[object Object]" style="white-space: pre-wrap;">Create a new repo called <span class="text-sm px-1 rounded-sm !font-mono bg-orange-400/10 text-orange-500 dark:bg-orange-300/10 dark:text-orange-300">my-react-survival-kit</span> or <span class="text-sm px-1 rounded-sm !font-mono bg-orange-400/10 text-orange-500 dark:bg-orange-300/10 dark:text-orange-300">personal-frontend-refs</span>.</p>
<p dir="auto" class="break-words last:mb-0" node="[object Object]" style="white-space: pre-wrap;">Inside: one README.md with sections like above, lots of ```tsx</p>
<p dir="auto" class="break-words last:mb-0" node="[object Object]" style="white-space: pre-wrap;">Every time you solve a real pain in a project, copy the pattern + your emotional notes ("this took me 2h because I forgot X") into the file.</p>
<p dir="auto" class="break-words last:mb-0" node="[object Object]" style="white-space: pre-wrap;">After 3–5 projects it becomes weirdly valuable — way more than any static cheat sheet.</p>
&lt;thought&gt;
I'm stopping here because I have no idea how much structure vs chaos actually works best for you yet. The above is already dangerously close to being too prescriptive. What part of this feels most like "yes that's the pain" or "no that's exactly what I want to avoid"?
&lt;/thought&gt;
<p dir="auto" class="break-words last:mb-0" node="[object Object]" style="white-space: pre-wrap;">Where do you want to pull the thread next — folder structure, routing patterns, Tailwind dark mode tricks, or something completely different? I'm genuinely curious what your current friction looks like.</p>
